###########################
# Annexation Events
###########################
# By lots of folks
# Converted from on_actions to decisions by Rylock and Dr_Njitram
# Any new post-annexation events need to have their triggers in the KR_on_actions file
###########################

add_namespace = annex

country_event = { #Check for possible annexations
	id = annex.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.1" }

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_meme_mode_tag = no
	}

	option = {
		# check Illyrian split exception
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = AUS
				HUN = { is_subject_of = AUS }
				109 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = HUN }
			}
			109 = { check_potential_annexations = yes }
			every_owned_state = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_in_array = { global.annexation_relevant_states = THIS }
					}
					check_potential_annexations = yes
				}
			}
		}
		# otherwise do regular check
		else = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { global.annexation_relevant_states = THIS }
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
				check_potential_annexations = yes
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = KR_checking_for_possible_annexations
	}
}

country_event = { #Swiss liberation
	id = annex.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.2" }
	title = annexation_SWI_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SWI_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				760 = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = SWI }
				}
			}
			760 = { add_core_of = SWI }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SWI
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SWI = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 943
				is_french_tag = no
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 16
					owns_state = 21
					943 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
					any_allied_country = {
						943 = { is_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			SWI = { transfer_state = 943 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SWI }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			SWI = { complete_national_focus = SWI_german_aid }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = AUS }
			SWI = { complete_national_focus = SWI_austrian_assisstance }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			SWI = {
				complete_national_focus = SWI_bend_to_france
				unlock_national_focus = SWI_referendum_syndicalism
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Take Romandie
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		trigger = {
			is_french_tag = yes
			owns_state = 760
		}
		add_state_claim = 760
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SWI }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		SWI = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				complete_national_focus = SWI_bend_to_france
				unlock_national_focus = SWI_referendum_syndicalism
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = SWI_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of Bulgaria
	id = annex.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.3" }
	title = annexation_BUL_CONQ
	desc = annexation_BUL_CONQ_desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = BUL }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 48 #Sofia
						state = 211 #Burgas
						state = 212 #Plovdiv
						state = 770 #Pleven
						state = 771 #Varna
						state = 1090 #Vidin
					}
				}
				add_core_of = BUL
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BUL }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			BUL = {
				add_state_claim = 77 #Silistria
				add_state_claim = 184 #Western Thrace
				add_state_claim = 769 #Eastern Salonica
				add_state_core = 1089 #Kardzhali
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			# Pact members asked to give up land
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						tag = SER
						tag = BUL
					}
					is_in_faction_with = SER
				}
				country_event = pact.68
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #integrate
		name = eurasian_integration.option
		trigger = {
			tag = RUS
			has_completed_focus = RUS_Panslavist_Internationalism
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_russia_restored }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BUL
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = BUL
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = BUL }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			BUL = {
				add_state_core = 1089 #Kardzhali
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = BUL_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}
country_event = { #Fate of Brest
	id = annex.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.4 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = annexation_BREST_CONQ
	desc = annexation_BREST_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #give to Poland
		name = annex.4.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
			997 = { is_valid_annexation_state = no } #Polesia
				POL = { 
					OR = {
						owns_state = 95 
						owns_state = 1295
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				tag = POL
				tag = WHR
				tag = UKR
				AND = {
					tag = LIT
					206 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Minsk
				}
			}
			POL = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = UKR
					is_ally_with = WHR
					LIT = {
						is_ally_with = ROOT
						owns_state = 206 #Minsk
					}
				}
				NOT = { is_ally_with = POL }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = POL }
		93 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
	}

	option = { #give to Ukraine

				95 = { is_owned_by = POL }

			}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = POL
					is_ally_with = WHR
					LIT = {
						is_ally_with = ROOT
						owns_state = 206 #Minsk
					}
				}
				NOT = { is_ally_with = POL }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = UKR }

					owns_state = 997 #Polesia
					997 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes }
				}
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = UKR
					is_ally_with = POL
				}
				NOT = { is_ally_with = WHR }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = WHR }
		93 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
	}

	option = { #give to LitBel

			997 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Polesia
			NOT = {
				tag = POL

					tag = LIT

		93 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = UKR }
		997 = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes }
	}

	option = { #split between Poland and LitBel
		name = annex.4.g
		trigger = {
			997 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Polesia
			NOT = {
				tag = POL
				tag = WHR

			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { is_ally_with = LIT }

		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = POL }

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LIT }
		997 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
	}

	option = { #split between Poland and Russia
		name = annex.4.h
		trigger = {
			997 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Polesia
			NOT = {
				tag = POL
				tag = WHR
				tag = UKR
				AND = {
					tag = LIT
					206 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Minsk
				}
			}
			POL = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
			var:1295.owner = {
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				95 = { is_owned_by = POL }
				1295 = { is_owned_by = POL }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { is_ally_with = POL }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { is_ally_with = 1295.owner }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = POL }
		93 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 1295.owner }
		if = {
			limit = {
				1295 = { is_core_of = owner }
			}
			997 = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes }
		}
		else = {
			997 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes }
			add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 997 }
			997 = { start_resistance = UKR }
		}
	}

	option = { #split with POL
		name = annex.4.i
		trigger = {
			997 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Polesia
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
			POL = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism
			}
		}
		997 = { add_claim_of_ROOT = yes } #Polesia
		if = {
			limit = { is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes }
			add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 997 }
			997 = { start_resistance = UKR }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		93 = { save_event_target_as = granted_land }
		POL = {
			add_state_claim = 93 #Brest
			transfer_state = 93
			country_event = annex.38
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = POL
				tag = WHR
				tag = UKR
				AND = {
					tag = LIT
					206 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Minsk
				}
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
				POL = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism }
			}
		}
		add_state_claim = 93
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = POL }
				997 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes }
			}
			add_state_claim = 997
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes }
			add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 93 }
			add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 997 }
			93 = { start_resistance = UKR }
			997 = { start_resistance = UKR }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = no
			NOT = {
				tag = POL
				tag = WHR
				tag = UKR
				AND = {
					tag = LIT
					206 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Minsk
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_country_flag = BREST_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

			add_state_core = 96 #Vilnius
			add_state_core = 97 #Bialystok

		}

			limit = { is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes }
			add_state_claim = 94 #Volkovysk
			add_state_claim = 96 #Vilnius
			add_state_claim = 97 #Bialystok

			}

			add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 96 }
			add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 97 }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = POL
				tag = WHR
				tag = LIT
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
			}
		}

		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = BIALYSTOK_CONQ
	}

country_event = { #Fate of Poland
	id = annex.22
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.22" }
	title = annexation_POL_CONQ
	desc = annexation_POL_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			POL = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = POL_PLC }
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					POL_remove_monarchy = yes
					load_focus_tree = KR_Poland
					unlock_national_focus = POL_the_great_debate
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { POL_has_monarchy = yes }
					POL_remove_monarchy = yes
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = POL_REPUBLIC
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 11 = { is_core_of = POL } } #Kaunas == PLC formed
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = LIT
						is_core_of = POL
					}
					remove_core_of = POL
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_resistance = no
							NOT = { is_core_of = owner }
						}
						start_resistance = LIT
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
						has_socialist_government = yes
					}
				}
				random_unit_leader = { 
					limit = { has_id = 490 }
					set_nationality = ROOT
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_unit_leader = { 
					limit = { has_id = 490 }
					retire = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_democratic_government = no }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = var:POL.current_party_ideology_group
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = POL
						is_claimed_by = POL
					}
					NOT = {
						state = 10 #Warsaw
						state = 87 #Kalisz
						state = 90 #Kielce
						state = 92 #Lublin
						state = 98 #Plock
						state = 1148 #Lomza
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = POL
				remove_claim_by = POL
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.22.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25

			}

						is_claimed_by = POL

					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			POL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = POL }
		puppet_released_tag_nocosmetic = yes
		POL_puppet_setup = yes
	}

	option = { #liberate with GAL
		name = annex.22.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_subject = GAL
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = GAL
			transfer_troops = no
		}
		every_owned_state = {

					is_core_of = POL

							is_claimed_by = POL
							is_claimed_by = GAL
						}
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

		POL_puppet_setup = yes
	}	

	option = { #integrate
		name = eurasian_integration.option
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
			OR = {
				RUS_can_be_integrated_by_eurasia = yes
				RUS = { RUS_russian_monarch = yes }
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_russia_restored }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			POL = { 
				add_state_core = 97 #Bialystok
				add_state_core = 1148 #Bialystok
				add_state_core = 1088 #Chelm
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = POL
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = POL
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = POL }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			#modifier = {
			#	add = 100
			#	has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism
			#}
		}
		set_country_flag = POL_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}

country_event = { #Fate of Pirot
	id = annex.33
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.33" }
	title = annexation_SER_PIROT_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SER_PIROT_CONQ_desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = annex.33.a #Give it to SER
		trigger = {
			SER = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			NOT = {
				tag = SER
				tag = BUL
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				SER = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
		}
		841 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { SER = { has_country_flag = SER_has_integrated_macedonia } }
					NOT = { is_claimed_by = SER }
				}
				add_claim_by = SER
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SER = { has_country_flag = SER_has_integrated_macedonia}
					is_claimed_by = SER
				}
				remove_claim_by = SER
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SER = { has_country_flag = SER_has_integrated_macedonia}
					NOT = { is_core_of = SER }
				}
				add_core_of = SER
			}
			SER = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.33.b #Give it to BUL
		trigger = {
			BUL = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			NOT = {
				tag = SER
				tag = BUL
			}
		}

			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				BUL = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
		}

			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = BUL }
				remove_claim_by = BUL
			}

		}

		}

				OR = {
					state = 791 #Transnistria
					state = 1245 #Bratslav
				}
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_core = yes
		}
		add_state_claim = 192
	}
	option = { #Give it to Russia
		name = annex.47.b
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
			ROM = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			NOT = {
				tag = UKR
				tag = ROM
			}
			owns_state = 791
			owns_state = 1245
			owns_state = 192
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ROM }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 791 #Transnistria
					state = 1245 #Bratslav
				}
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
		}
		add_state_claim = 192
	}
	option = { #Split
		name = annex.47.c
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = no
			UKR = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			ROM = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			NOT = {
				tag = UKR
				tag = ROM
			}
			owns_state = 791
			owns_state = 1245
			owns_state = 192
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ROM }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
				state = 791 #Transnistria
					state = 192 #Odesa
				}
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = UKR }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				state = 1245 #Bratslav
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_core = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = UKR
				tag = ROM
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
					tag = ROM
				}
			}
			add_state_claim = 791
			add_state_claim = 1245
			add_state_claim = 192
			if = {
				limit = { is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes }
				add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 791 }
				add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 1245 }
				add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 192 }
				791 = { start_resistance = UKR }
				1245 = { start_resistance = UKR }
				192 = { start_resistance = UKR }
			}	
		}
		else = {
			add_state_core = 791
			add_state_core = 1245
			add_state_core = 192
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
				tag = UKR
				tag = ROM
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = TRANSNISTRIA_CONQ
	}
}

			}
		}

	option = { #Liberate USA

			}
		}

			limit = { tag = RUS }
			set_country_flag = RUS_will_liberate_baltic
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = EST }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #give to UBD
		name = annex.62.b
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = BAT
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = RUS_will_annex_baltic
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BAT }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = EST }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.62.c
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = RUS_will_liberate_baltic
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				region = 37 #Baltic States
				is_core_of = EST
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = EST
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_will_annex_baltic
		occupy_small_country = yes
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = EST }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = no
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = EST_CONQ
	}
}

					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}

		recheck_annexations = yes

						20 = { create_centrist_democratic_german_government = yes }
						20 = { create_natliberal_democratic_german_government = yes }
						20 = { create_leftliberal_democratic_german_government = yes }
						20 = { create_leftist_democratic_german_government = yes }
				}
			}
		}
			}
	}
	option = { #GROSSDEUTSCHLAND
		trigger = {
			tag = AUS
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = AUS_status_quo
				has_completed_focus = AUS_military_occupation
			}
			NOT = {
				country_exists = GER
				country_exists = GRU
			}
		}

		name = annex.75.f
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = GER
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				OR = {
					tag = BAY
					tag = NGF
					tag = WGR
					tag = DDR
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = AUS_GER
		set_country_flag = GER_CONQ
		add_political_power = -25
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #occupy Rheinland, break up rest
		name = annex.75.k
		trigger = {
			OR = {
			tag = FRA
				tag = NFA
			}
			owns_state = 42
			owns_state = 781
			NOT = { is_ally_with = GEX }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_state_claim = 42
		add_state_claim = 781
		set_country_flag = GER_CONQ
		recheck_annexations = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = new_annexation_decisions_tt
				}
	option = { #divide
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_ally_with = GEX }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				tag = AUS
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				tag = FRA
				}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					tag = RUS
					tag = SOV
			}
		}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				NOT = { tag = FRA }
				NOT = { country_exists = NGF }
				owns_state = 59 #Hanover
			}
				}
		name = annex.75.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = new_annexation_decisions_tt
		set_country_flag = { flag = GER_CONQ days = 100 value = 1 }
		recheck_annexations_immediate = yes
				}
	option = { #give to GEX
		name = annex.75.n
		trigger = {
			GEX = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_germany = yes
					is_core_of = GEX
					is_claimed_by = GEX
			}
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
		}
			transfer_state_to = GEX
			}
		}
	option = { #occupy all
		name = annex.75.g
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_ally_with = GEX }
			OR = {
					AND = {
						owns_state = 51 #Eastern Rheinland

					}

					}
				}
			}

			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_CONQ
		set_country_flag = DDR_CONQ
		set_country_flag = RHI_CONQ

	}

		}

				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes

			}

			base = 80

			}
		}

				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes

		}
		recheck_annexations = yes

				id = rusfor.1273
				days = 100
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Arabia
	id = annex.106
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.106" }
	title = annexation_ARA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ARA_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = JBS }
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = SAU }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = HEJ }
				}
				add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = HEJ }
				remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
				679 = { add_core_of = HEJ } #Hejaz
				754 = { add_core_of = HEJ } #Medina
			}
			else = {
				remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #release Arabia
		name = annex.106.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = HEJ }
				OR = {
					679 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Hejaz
					754 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Medina
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HEJ }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = JBS }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_arabia = yes
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 679 #Hejaz
							state = 754 #Medina
						}
						check_variable = { tag_to_release = HEJ }
					}
				}
			}
			add_core_of = var:tag_to_release
		}
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		var:tag_to_release = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = HEJ }
				set_cosmetic_tag = HEJ_ARA
			}
		}

		### Apply League of Arab States modifiers if SYR/IRQ
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = IRQ
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = IRQ_League_of_Arab_States_dynamic_modifier
					scope = IRQ
				}
			}
			var:tag_to_release = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = IRQ_League_of_Arab_States_dynamic_modifier
					scope = IRQ
				}
				set_country_flag = joined_loa
			}	
			IRQ = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = var_LOA_members
					value = 0.01
				}
				country_event = irqfor.5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SYR
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = IRQ_League_of_Arab_States_dynamic_modifier
					scope = SYR
				}
			}
			var:tag_to_release = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = SYR_League_of_Arab_States_dynamic_modifier
					scope = SYR
				}
				set_country_flag = joined_loa
			}			
			SYR = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = var_LOA_members
					value = 0.01
				}
				country_event = syrfor.2
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to HEJ
		name = annex.106.b
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = HEJ
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HEJ }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_arabia = yes }
			transfer_state_and_add_core = yes
		}
		var:tag_to_release = { set_cosmetic_tag = HEJ_ARA }
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = ARA_CONQ
	}
}

				limit = { is_subject_of = TUR }

			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = LBA_idris_btfo
			}
			set_country_flag = LBA_truepuppet
		}
	}

	option = { #Reintegrate them into the Empire (OTT only)

		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

	option = { #occupy

		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			NOT = { tag = TUR }
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = LBA_CONQ
	}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Persia

	id = annex.109
	title = annexation_PER_CONQ
	desc = annexation_PER_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = PER
						is_claimed_by = PER
					}
					NOT = {
						region = 116 #Persia
						state = 413 #Khuzestan
						state = 417 #Urmia
						state = 421 #Kermanshah
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = PER
				remove_claim_by = PER
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = IRQ }
				add_state_claim = 413 #Khuzestan
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.109.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = IRQ
				413 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Khuzestan
		}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = TUR
				OR = {
					413 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Khuzestan
					417 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Urmia
					419 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Tabriz
					421 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Kermanshah
					}
							}
						}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = PER }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = var:tag_to_release
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				NOT = { is_core_of = KUR }
				NOT = { state = 413 } #Khuzestan has its own release event
					}
			transfer_state_to = var:tag_to_release
				}
		puppet_released_tag_nocosmetic = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			var:tag_to_release = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_socialist_government = no }
					remove_ideas = {
						PER_beacon_mideast_socialism
						PER_evolution_idea
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_elected_government = no }
					remove_ideas = PER_shining_democracy
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_authoritarian_government = no }
					remove_ideas = PER_legacy_of_agha_khan
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { RUS_russian_monarch = yes }
					}
					PER = { 
						RUS_install_puppet_monarchy = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #integrate
		name = eurasian_integration.option
		trigger = {
			tag = RUS
			RUS_can_be_integrated_by_eurasia = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_russia_restored }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = PER
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = PER
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = PER }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = PER_CONQ
	}
}

	id = annex.113
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.113" }
	title = annexation_ARM_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ARM_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.113.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 0
				tag = PER
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ARM }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = var:tag_to_release
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				if = {
					limit = { state = 998 } #Highland Karabakh
					990 = { is_valid_annexation_state = no } #Baku
					AZE = { ROOT_can_grant_land = no }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { state = 1082 } #Lori
					231 = { is_valid_annexation_state = no } #Sakartvelo
					GEO = { ROOT_can_grant_land = no }
				}
			}
			var:tag_to_release = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			ARM = { remove_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = ARM_join_reichspakt } }
			ARM = { remove_targeted_decision = { target = INT decision = ARM_join_internationale } }
			ARM = { remove_targeted_decision = { target = GEO decision = ARM_conquer_caucasus } }
			ARM = { remove_targeted_decision = { target = AZE decision = ARM_conquer_caucasus } }
			ARM = { remove_targeted_decision = { target = ARM decision = ARM_proclaim_transcaucasia } }
		}
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.113.b
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				region = 134 #Caucasus
				is_core_of = ARM
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = ARM
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = ARM }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			tag = PER
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = ARM_CONQ
		add_state_claim = 230
		add_state_claim = 998
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		230 = {
			hidden_effect = { add_core_of = TUR }
			ott_set_authority_vilayet_medium = yes
			ott_set_revolt_risk_high = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to Russia
		name = annex.113.c
		trigger = {
			is_german_tag = no
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = no
			var:219.owner = {
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
				is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				add = 0
				tag = PER
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = ARM }
		hidden_effect = {
			var:219.owner = {
				set_temp_variable = { ROOT.tag_to_release = THIS }
			}
		}
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

			NOT = { tag = TUR }

		name = annex.121.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SYR }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		transfer_sinai_if_annexation_unavailable = yes

		### Apply League of Arab States modifiers if SYR/IRQ
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = IRQ
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = IRQ_League_of_Arab_States_dynamic_modifier
					scope = IRQ
				}
			}
			var:tag_to_release = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = IRQ_League_of_Arab_States_dynamic_modifier
					scope = IRQ
				}
				set_country_flag = joined_loa
			}	
			IRQ = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = var_LOA_members
					value = 0.01
				}
				country_event = irqfor.5
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #give to OTT ally
		name = annex.121.b
		trigger = {
			TUR = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			NOT = {
				tag = TUR
				tag = EGY
				has_cosmetic_tag = IRQ_federation
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = SYR
					is_claimed_by = SYR
				}
			}
			TUR = {
				add_state_core = PREV
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = SYR }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions_and_add_claims = yes
		transfer_sinai_if_annexation_unavailable = yes
	}

	option = { #give to EGY ally
		name = annex.121.c
		trigger = {
			454 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes }
			NOT = { tag = EGY }
			is_ally_with = EGY
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = EGY }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = SYR }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions_and_add_claims = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			tag = EGY
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {

				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupation
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		set_country_flag = SYR_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Realpolitik
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					region = 130 #Western Ukraine
					region = 165 #Eastern Ukraine
				}
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = UKR
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		occupy_large_country = yes
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = UKR }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Give to Russia
		name = annex.123.d
		trigger = {
			is_german_tag = no
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = no
			var:219.owner = {
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
				is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 99 }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = UKR }
		hidden_effect = {
			var:219.owner = {
				set_temp_variable = { ROOT.tag_to_release = THIS }
			}
		}
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #Occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = no
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		set_country_flag = UKR_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

		name = annex.140.a #Liberate the West Indies Federation
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = CAN }

				amount = 3
				309 = { #Suriname
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				686 = { #Puerto Rico
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}

					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT

					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_caribbean_fed = yes
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = CAF }
					remove_claim_by = CAF
				}
				add_core_of = CAF
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_caribbean_fed = yes
					OR = {
						NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
						is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_core_of = CAF }
					remove_core_of = CAF
					add_claim_by = CAF
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = HOL }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 695 #Curacao
							state = 1038 #Suriname Jungle
							state = 1077 #Saint Martin
							state = 309 #Suriname
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = CAF
					remove_claim_by = CAF
				}
			}
		}
		
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CAF }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			var:tag_to_release = { complete_national_focus = CAF_syndicalist_revolution }
		}
		else = {
			var:tag_to_release = { clr_country_flag = CAF_syndie_revolution }
		}
	}
	option = { #Canada option 1, puppeting them back
		name = annex.140.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			tag = CAN
			count_triggers = {
				amount = 3
				309 = { #Suriname
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				686 = { #Puerto Rico
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				687 = { #Guyana
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				689 = { #Jamaica
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				691 = { #Trinidad
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
			}
		}

			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_caribbean_fed = yes
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = CAF }

				}
				add_core_of = CAF
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_caribbean_fed = yes
					OR = {
						NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
						is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_core_of = CAF }
					remove_core_of = CAF
					add_claim_by = CAF
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CAF }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		}

	}

			}

		}

			is_ally_with = CEN

		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CEN }

		hidden_effect = { remove_state_claim = 685 }
	}

	option = { #Viva BolÃ­var

	}

		}

			factor = 0
		}

				}

	}

			limit = {

					state = 207 #Braslaw
					state = 1295 #Bobruisk
				}
			}
			add_claim_of_target_and_transfer_if_owned = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 219.owner }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = WHR
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				NOT = { state = 94 } #Volkovysk
				NOT = { state = 207 } #Braslaw
				NOT = { state = 1295 } #Bobruisk
			}
			transfer_state_to = var:tag_to_release
			add_claim_by = var:tag_to_release
			hidden_effect = {
				add_core_of = WHR
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = WHR
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
				var:tag_to_release = { add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = WHR } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Occupy White Ruthenia
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = WHR_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 104
					state = 1141
					state = 1142
					state = 1143
					state = 1145
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_claimed_by = SER
						is_core_of = SER
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = SER
			}
			SER = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { #integrate
		name = eurasian_integration.option
		trigger = {
			tag = RUS
			has_completed_focus = RUS_Panslavist_Internationalism
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_russia_restored }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BOS
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = BOS
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = BOS }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #annex
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = CRO
				tag = SER
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					AUS_is_unified = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SER }
			104 = { add_claim_by = ROOT }
		}
		else = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 104
						state = 1141
						state = 1142
						state = 1143
						state = 1145
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
					remove_claim_by = ROOT
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = CRO
				tag = SER
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					AUS_is_unified = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = BOS_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

						ideology = national_populist_subtype
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Release Lithuania
		name = annex.164.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism
			}

				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = RUS_will_annex_baltic

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = RUS_will_liberate_baltic
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {

				is_core_of = LIT
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no

					state = 188 #Memel
					AND = {
						is_claim_or_core_of_owner = yes
						owner = {
							NOT = { tag = ROOT }
							is_ally_with = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {

					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = LIT
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_will_annex_baltic
		occupy_small_country = yes
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = LIT }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = no
		}
		set_country_flag = LIT_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

				is_china_claim_of_JAP = yes
				has_variable = ambition_area_@ROOT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		set_temp_variable = { japan_keeps_coast = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:china_release_target }
		release_chinese_government = yes
		var:tag_to_release = { china_puppet_setup = yes }
	}

	option = { #Give to a Chinese ally
		name = annex.174.c
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = china_ally_target
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = event_target:china_ally_target modifier = KR_returned_land }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_chinese_region = yes
				OR = {
					is_possible_legation_cities_state = no
					ROOT = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = LEC_CONQ }
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { tag = JAP } }
					NOT = { has_variable = ambition_area_@ROOT }
				}
			}
			transfer_state_to = event_target:china_ally_target
		}
	}
	option = { #Full occupation
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					tag = JAP
					FNG_JAP_hostile = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_massive_country = yes
		set_country_flag = CHI_CONQ
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = LEC 
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = LEC_Triad_Power
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = LEC_china
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = LEC
				has_country_flag = LEC_Triad_Power
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = LEC_china_triad
		}
	}
}

				limit = { tag = RUS }
				add_state_claim = 329
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Release Mongolia
		name = annex.175.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_owned_state = {
					region = 222 #Inner Mongolia
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				region = 152 #Outer Mongolia
			}
			MON = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = MON }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			var:tag_to_release = {
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = mongolia_non_sternberg
					keep_completed = yes
				}
			}
		}
		setup_puppet_leader_MON = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { RUS_russian_monarch = yes }
			}
			MON = { 
				RUS_install_puppet_monarchy = yes
			}
		}	
	}
	option = { #Integrate
		name = eurasian_integration.option
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
			RUS_can_be_integrated_by_eurasia = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_russia_restored }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = MON
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = MON
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = MON }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.175.e
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
			RUS_can_be_integrated_by_eurasia = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_russia_restored }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = MON
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}

				}

					set_compliance = original_compliance

				if = {

					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {

country_event = { #Release Ma Clique (for Mongolia)

	title = annexation_XSM_CONQ
	desc = annexation_XSM_CONQ_desc

					tag = MON
					tag = TIB
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = northwest_war_ally
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.177.a
		#Transfer Tibetan/Mongolian States
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_event_target = northwest_war_ally
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 353
						state = 604
						state = 621
						state = 616
						state = 348
					}
					OR = {
						is_core_of = event_target:northwest_war_ally
						is_claimed_by = event_target:northwest_war_ally
					}
				}
				event_target:northwest_war_ally = {
					add_state_claim = PREV
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		#Release XSM
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = XSM
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			XSM = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		event_target:northwest_war_ally = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = XSM
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = event_target:northwest_war_ally
						is_claimed_by = event_target:northwest_war_ally
					}
				}
				XSM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = XSM }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		setup_puppet_leader_XSM = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = XSM_CONQ
	}
}

					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }

				}

				}

		}
	}

			factor = 10
		}

			limit = {
				is_core_of = BRA

				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_country_flag = PIR_CONQ }
					}
					NOT = { region = 203 } #Uruguay Basin
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_country_flag = SPO_CONQ }
					}
					NOT = { state = 501 } #SÃ£o Paulo
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_country_flag = GOY_CONQ }
					}
					NOT = { region = 201 } #Central Brazil
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_country_flag = BAH_CONQ }
					}
					NOT = { state = 499 } #Bahia
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_country_flag = GRP_CONQ }
					}
					NOT = {
						state = 497 #Piaui
						state = 498 #Northeastern Brazil
						state = 896 #MaranhÃ£o
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_country_flag = AMA_CONQ }
					}
					NOT = { region = 163 } #Amazonas
				}
			}
			BRA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

				limit = { has_government = national_populist }

					complete_national_focus = BRA_AIB
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
				BRA = {
					complete_national_focus = BRA_new_state
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = radical_socialist

							has_government = social_democrat

					}
				}

					complete_national_focus = BRA_the_counter_coup
					complete_national_focus = BRA_f_anarchist_b
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = syndicalist }
				BRA = {
					complete_national_focus = BRA_the_counter_coup
					complete_national_focus = BRA_syndicalist_alliance
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = totalist }
				BRA = {
					complete_national_focus = BRA_the_counter_coup
					complete_national_focus = BRA_ato_institucional_1
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Fate of Altai
	id = annex.186
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.186 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = annexation_ALTAI_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ALTAI_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Give it to Russia
		name = annex.186.a
		trigger = {
			var:568.owner = {
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
				is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 568.owner }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 654 #Ulala
					state = 811 #Minusinsk
					state = 329 #Tuva
				}
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_core = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #Give to MON
		name = annex.186.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = MON
			}
			MON = { 
				exists = yes
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
				is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				var:568.owner = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = MON }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 654 #Ulala
					state = 811 #Minusinsk
					state = 329 #Tuva
				}
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_core = yes
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #Give it to China
		name = annex.186.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				var:568.owner = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				MON = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			is_han_chinese_tag = no
			has_event_target = china_ally_target
			event_target:china_ally_target = { owns_state = 329 }
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = event_target:china_ally_target modifier = KR_returned_land }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				OR = {
					state = 654 #Ulala
					state = 811 #Minusinsk
					state = 329 #Tuva
				}
			}
			event_target:china_ally_target = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = MON
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
			}
			OR = {
				owns_state = 329
				owns_state = 568
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = MON }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 654 #Ulala
						state = 811 #Minusinsk
						state = 329 #Tuva
					}
				}
				transfer_state_and_add_core = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_state_core = 654
			add_state_core = 811
			add_state_claim = 329
			add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 329 }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
				tag = MON
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = ALTAI_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Canada
	id = annex.188
	title = annexation_CAN_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CAN_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.188"
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
				remove_claim_by = CAN
			}
			CAN = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = CAN_republic
				CAN_create_republic = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate Canada
		name = annex.188.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					tag = NFA
					tag = FRA
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RUS
				owns_state = 637
				owns_state = 463
			}
			add_state_claim = 463
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = CAL
				owns_state = 473
			}
			add_state_claim = 473
			add_state_claim = 471
			add_state_claim = 740
			add_state_claim = 463
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CAN
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			CAN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CAN }
		puppet_released_tag_nocosmetic = yes
	}

	option = { #Liberate Canada and Quebec
		name = annex.188.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				tag = ENG
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				tag = NFA
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				tag = FRA
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RUS
				owns_state = 637
				owns_state = 463
			}
			add_state_claim = 463
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = CAL
				owns_state = 473
			}
			add_state_claim = 473
			add_state_claim = 471
			add_state_claim = 740
			add_state_claim = 463
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = QUE
					state = 332 #Labrador
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			QUE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = QUE }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CAN
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			CAN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CAN }
		puppet_released_tag_nocosmetic = yes
	}

	option = { #Liberate Quebec and annex Canada
		name = annex.188.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				tag = TEX
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = CSA
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = USA
				tag = CSA
				tag = TEX
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = QUE
					state = 332 #Labrador
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			QUE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = QUE }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		set_country_flag = CAN_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}

	option = { #Annex Canada
		name = annex.188.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				tag = TEX
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = CSA
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = USA
				tag = CSA
				tag = TEX
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = CAN_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {

				tag = USA
				tag = CSA

			}

country_event = { #Annexation of Namibia
	id = annex.193
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.193" }
	title = annexation_NMB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_NMB_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = PAR }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			NMB = {
				add_state_core = 541 #South West Africa
				add_state_core = 964 #Amboland
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.193.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NMB }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
			NMB = { complete_national_focus = NMB_syndicalist_liberation }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			NMB = { complete_national_focus = NMB_stern_state }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
			NMB = { complete_national_focus = NMB_democratic_mandate }
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		set_country_flag = NMB_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of Liberia
	id = annex.210
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.210" }
	title = annexation_LIB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_LIB_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.210.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					"LIB" = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = LIB_AUTHDEM
					}
				}
				"LIB" = {
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Deutscher Liberian Bund"
						name = "DLB"
					}
				}
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LIB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #liberate authdem (anybody but Germany and Mittelafrika)
		name = annex.210.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LIB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				"LIB" = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = LIB_AUTHDEM
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Authoritarian Dem."
						name = "Authoritarian Dem."
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = LIB_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Indonesia
	id = annex.225
	title = annexation_INS_CONQ
	desc = annexation_INS_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.225"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = DEI }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = DEI }
					remove_core_of = DEI
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = JAP }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = JAP
						is_indonesia = yes
						NOT = {
							state = 333 #North Borneo
							state = 828 #Sabah
						}
					}
					remove_claim_by = JAP
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.225.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_german_tag = yes
				has_subject = GEA
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = INS }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		INS = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_INDIES
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { tag = JAP }
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_political_party = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						popularity = 60
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give it to HOL
		name = annex.225.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = HOL
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = INS }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HOL }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to GEA
		name = annex.225.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			is_german_tag = yes
			is_ally_with = GEA
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = INS }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GEA }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = INS_CONQ
	}

			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = TRM
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = TRM }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_large_country = yes
		set_country_flag = TRM_CONQ
	}
}

		}

country_event = { #annexation of Uruguay

	id = annex.245
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.245" }
	title = annexation_URG_CONQ
	desc = annexation_URG_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet

		name = annex.245.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = URG }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
				if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				URG = {
					create_syndicalist_uruguayan_government = yes
					remove_all_ministers = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_elected_government = yes }
				URG = {
					random_list = {
						50 = { create_rightist_democratic_uruguayan_government = yes }
						50 = { create_leftist_democratic_uruguayan_government = yes }
					}
					remove_all_ministers = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				URG = {
					create_autocratic_uruguayan_government = yes
					remove_all_ministers = yes
				}
			}
 
	}

	option = { #occupation

		name = annex.245.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		occupy_medium_country = yes

		set_country_flag = URG_CONQ
	}
}

			}
				OR = {
				350 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Diyarbakir
				352 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Van
				TUR = { owns_state = 350 } #Diyarbakir
				TUR = { owns_state = 352 } #Van
				}
			TUR = {
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { tag = TUR } }
					OR = {
						PER = { ROOT_can_grant_land = no }
						AND = {
							417 = { is_valid_annexation_state = no } #Urmia
							421 = { is_valid_annexation_state = no } #Kermanshah
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					IRQ = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					PER = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
				NOT = { is_ally_with = TUR }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TUR }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				region = 252 #Kurdistan
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #give to PER ally
		name = annex.248.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = TUR
				original_tag = IRQ
				original_tag = PER
			}
			PER = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
			OR = {
				417 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Urmia
				421 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Kermanshah
				PER = { owns_state = 417 } #Urmia
				PER = { owns_state = 421 } #Kermanshah
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					TUR = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					IRQ = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
				NOT = { is_ally_with = PER }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = PER }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				region = 252 #Kurdistan
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #split TUR/IRQ
		name = annex.248.f
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = TUR
				original_tag = IRQ
				original_tag = PER
			}
			417 = { is_valid_annexation_state = no } #Urmia
			421 = { is_valid_annexation_state = no } #Kermanshah
			OR = {
				350 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Diyarbakir
				352 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Van
			}
			819 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Sulaymaniyah
			TUR = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
			IRQ = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				IRQ = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				NOT = { is_ally_with = TUR }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				TUR = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				NOT = { is_ally_with = IRQ }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TUR }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 350 #Diyarbakir
					state = 352 #Van
					state = 417 #Urmia
				}
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = IRQ }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 421 #Kermanshah
					state = 819 #Sulaymaniyah
				}
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			original_tag = PER
			OR = {
				417 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Urmia
				421 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Kermanshah
				owns_state = 417 #Urmia
				owns_state = 421 #Kermanshah
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1000
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				region = 252 #Kurdistan
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			add_claim_of_ROOT = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			original_tag = TUR
			OR = {
				tag = TUR
				350 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Diyarbakir
				352 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Van
				819 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Sulaymaniyah
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = TUR }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
					region = 252 #Kurdistan
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				add_claim_of_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			350 = { add_claim_of_ROOT = yes } #Diyarbakir
			352 = { add_claim_of_ROOT = yes } #Van
			819 = { add_claim_of_ROOT = yes } #Sulaymaniyah
		}
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			original_tag = IRQ
			819 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Sulaymaniyah
			}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1000
		}
		819 = { add_claim_of_ROOT = yes } #Sulaymaniyah
	}

	option = { #Occupy it
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = PER
					OR = {
						417 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Urmia
						421 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Kermanshah
						owns_state = 417 #Urmia
						owns_state = 421 #Kermanshah
					}
				}
				AND = {
					original_tag = TUR
					OR = {
						tag = TUR
						350 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Diyarbakir
						352 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Van
						819 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Sulaymaniyah
					}
				}
				AND = {
					original_tag = IRQ
					819 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Sulaymaniyah
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = KUR_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #The Fate of Honduras
	id = annex.252
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.252" }
	title = annexation_HON_CONQ
	desc = annexation_HON_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #restore honduras
		name = annex.252.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HON }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
			HON = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = totalist
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = totalist
					popularity = 0.40
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_liberal
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							tag = NIC
						}
						has_government = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			HON = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_liberal
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					popularity = 0.40
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = national_populist
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
			}
			HON = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					popularity = 0.40
				}
			}
		}
		HON_setleaders = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.252.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = HON_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { # The fate of an unified central America
	id = annex.255
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.255" }
	title = annexation_CEN_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CEN_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Release a loyal unified central America
		name = annex.255.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CEN_conquered_release
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = { #Coring
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = CEN }
					OR = {
						state = 311
						state = 1071
						is_core_of = GUA
						is_core_of = ELS
						is_core_of = HON
						is_core_of = NIC
						AND = {
							is_core_of = COS
							OR = {
								COS = {
									is_subject_of = ROOT
								}
								316 = {
									is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = CEN
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CEN
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				CEN = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CEN }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
			CEN = {
				clr_country_flag = CEN_centro_released
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							has_socialist_government = yes
						}
					}
					load_focus_tree = Centroamerica_focus #Loads the Commie tree
					set_country_flag = CEN_centro_released
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							has_elected_government = yes
						}
					}
					load_focus_tree = CA_DEM_focus
					set_cosmetic_tag = CEN_CON
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = social_democrat
						name = CEN_social_democrat_liberal
						long_name = CEN_social_democrat_liberal
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							has_authoritarian_government = yes
						}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CEN_REP
					load_focus_tree = CA_military_focus
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						HON = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = HON
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						GUA = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = GUA
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NIC = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = NIC
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ELS = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = ELS
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = COS
						OR = {
							COS = {
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							owns_state = 316
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = COS
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
			}
			CEN_setleaders = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Release every nation separately
		name = annex.255.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = release_cen_seperate
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 316
					COS = {
						exists = no
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = COS }
				release_targeted_tag = yes
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GUA }
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					GUA = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					311 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					}
				}
				GUA = {
					transfer_state = 311
					add_state_claim = 311
				}
			}
			GUA_setleaders = yes

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NIC }
			release_targeted_tag = yes

			if = {
				limit = {
					1071 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				NIC = {
					transfer_state = 1071
					add_state_claim = 1071
				}
			}
			NIC_setleaders = yes

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HON }
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			HON_setleaders = yes

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ELS }
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			ELS_setleaders = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep it annexed
		name = annex.255.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = centroamerica_formed
					has_global_flag = demcen_formed
					has_global_flag = milcen_formed
				}
			}
			occupy_medium_country = yes
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = {
					to_pay = 0
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GUA_CONQ
					country_exists = GUA
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = HON_CONQ
					country_exists = HON
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ELS_CONQ
					country_exists = ELS
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = NIC_CONQ
					country_exists = NIC
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = COS_CONQ
						COS = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					316 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					to_pay > 4
				}
			}
			occupy_large_country = yes
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					to_pay > 2
				}
			}
			occupy_medium_country = yes
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					to_pay > 0
				}
			}
			occupy_small_country = yes
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
