country_event = { #Fate of Constantinople
	id = annex.265
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.265" }
	title = annexation_CONSTANTINOPLE_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CONSTANTINOPLE_CONQ_DESC

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #transfer TUR/OTT
		name = annex.265.a
		trigger = {
			TUR = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
			NOT = {
				tag = GRE
				tag = TUR
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { is_ally_with = TUR }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TUR }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 773 #Constantinople
					state = 341 #Adrianople
				}
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			add_core_of_target_and_transfer_if_owned = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #transfer to GRE
		name = annex.265.b
		trigger = {
			GRE = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
			NOT = {
				tag = GRE
				tag = TUR
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { is_ally_with = GRE }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 773 #Constantinople
					state = 341 #Adrianople
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_claimed_by = GRE
						is_core_of = GRE
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = GRE
			}
			GRE = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { #transfer to BUL
		name = annex.265.c
		trigger = {
			BUL = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			NOT = {
				tag = GRE
				tag = BUL
				tag = TUR
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 773 #Constantinople
					state = 341 #Adrianople
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_claimed_by = BUL
						is_core_of = BUL
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = BUL
			}
			BUL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { #annex
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
				tag = TUR
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 773 #Constantinople
					state = 341 #Adrianople
				}
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			remove_claim_and_add_core_of_ROOT = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #annex
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GRE
				tag = BUL
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 773 #Constantinople
					state = 341 #Adrianople
				}
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
	}
	option = { #occupation
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			NOT = {
				tag = GRE
				tag = BUL
				tag = TUR
			}

	}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Rhineland
	id = annex.267
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.267" }
	title = annexation_WGR_CONQ
	desc = annexation_WGR_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { country_exists = WGR } }
				add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = WGR }
				remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						42 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Western Rhineland
						781 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Palatinate
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = controls_rhine_west_bank
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					51 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Eastern Rhineland
				}
				save_event_target_as = controls_rhine_east_bank
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.267.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = RHI
				GEX = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		create_rhenish_cores = yes
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = WGR }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					tag = SOV
					tag = FRA
				}
			}
			WGR = { country_event = part.52 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = RUS }
			WGR = { country_event = part.20 }
		}
		}
	option = { #give it to Germany
		name = annex.267.b
		trigger = {
			var:55.owner = {
				is_germany_or_splinter_tag = yes
				is_ally_with = ROOT
	}
			NOT = { is_ally_with = GEX }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				is_french_tag = yes
			}
			}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 55.owner }
		if = {
			limit = { var:tag_to_release = { original_tag = WGR } }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 42
						state = 51
						state = 55
						state = 57
						state = 781
		}
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
				transfer_state_to = var:tag_to_release
		}
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_rhineland = yes
						is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
		}
					add_core_of = var:tag_to_release
					transfer_state_to = var:tag_to_release
		}
				every_state = {
				limit = {
						is_rhineland = yes
						is_valid_annexation_state = no
				}
					add_claim_by = var:tag_to_release
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = { 
						is_rhineland = yes
		}
					add_core_and_transfer_if_owned_else_add_claim = yes
	}
		}
				}
			}
	
	option = { #occupy Rhineland, give the rest to Germany
		name = annex.267.c
		trigger = {
			is_french_tag = yes
			has_event_target = controls_rhine_west_bank
			var:55.owner = {
				is_germany_or_splinter_tag = yes
				is_ally_with = ROOT
			}
			NOT = { is_ally_with = GEX }
			}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		add_state_claim = 42
		add_state_claim = 781
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 55.owner }
		51 = { add_core_of_target_and_transfer_if_owned = yes }
	}
	option = { #occupy Rheinland, release rest
		name = annex.267.e
		trigger = {
			is_french_tag = yes
			has_event_target = controls_rhine_west_bank
			has_event_target = controls_rhine_east_bank
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_state_claim = 42
		add_state_claim = 781
		create_rhenish_cores = yes
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = WGR }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { tag = FRA	}
		WGR = { country_event = part.52 }
	}
	}
	
	option = { #occupy Rhineland
		name = annex.267.d
		trigger = {
			is_french_tag = yes
			has_event_target = controls_rhine_west_bank
			NOT = {
				has_event_target = controls_rhine_east_bank
				GEX = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		add_state_claim = 42
		add_state_claim = 781
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}

	option = { #give it to GEX
		name = annex.75.n
		trigger = {
			GEX = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				region = 6 #Rhineland
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			transfer_state_to = GEX
		}
	}
	
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_french_tag = no
				has_event_target = controls_rhine_east_bank
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { is_french_tag = yes }
			add_state_claim = 42
			add_state_claim = 781
		}
		occupy_large_country = yes
		set_country_flag = WGR_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Siberia
	id = annex.269
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.269" }
	title = annexation_SIB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SIB_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet

		name = annex.269.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = JAP
				NOT = { country_exists = TRM }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 408 #Vladivostok
						state = 1246 #Vladivostok
						state = 409 #Khabarovsk
						state = 560 #Nikolayevsk
						state = 562 #Okhotsk
						state = 637 #Kamchatka
					}
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				add_claim_by = JAP
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_russian_far_east = no
				OR = {
					is_siberia = yes
					is_core_of = SIB
					AND = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						OR = {
							state = 582 #Orsk
							state = 573 #Zlatoust
							state = 581 #Northern Urals
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { tag = JAP }
						OR = {
							state = 408 #Vladivostok
							state = 1246 #Vladivostok
							state = 409 #Khabarovsk
							state = 560 #Nikolayevsk
							state = 562 #Okhotsk
							state = 637 #Kamchatka
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 564 #Verkhneudinsk
					state = 563 #Chita
					state = 565 #Bodaybo
					state = 1208 #Orenburg
					state = 582 #Orsk
					state = 583 #Kustanai
					state = 590 #Akmolinsk
					state = 588 #Pavlodar
					state = 654 #Ulala
					state = 811 #Minusinsk
					state = 329 #Tuva
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SIB = {
				add_state_core = PREV
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SIB }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.269.c #give it to Transamur
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = TRM
				TRM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 300
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_siberia = yes
					AND = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						OR = {
							state = 582 #Orsk
							state = 573 #Zlatoust
							state = 581 #Northern Urals
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 564 #Verkhneudinsk
					state = 563 #Chita
					state = 565 #Bodaybo
					state = 1208 #Orenburg
					state = 582 #Orsk
					state = 583 #Kustanai
					state = 590 #Akmolinsk
					state = 588 #Pavlodar
					state = 654 #Ulala
					state = 811 #Minusinsk
					state = 329 #Tuva
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			TRM = {
				add_state_core = PREV
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy

		name = annex.269.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		occupy_large_country = yes

		set_country_flag = SIB_CONQ
	}

			}
			GYA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { #incorporate

			OR = {
				tag = CAF

			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes

				is_core_of = SUR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }

		hidden_effect = {

					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 783 #Trentino
							state = 39 #Southern Tyrol
							state = 736 #Austrian Littoral
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = ITA }
						remove_core_of = ITA

						remove_core_of = SRI

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.a #Release as Italy
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = {
				tag = AUS
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat

				ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					SIC = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					SRD = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}

		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_CONQ

			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ITA }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

			ITA = {
				if = {
					limit = {

					}
					add_ideas = ITA_republic_federation
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = national_populist

					}

				}

					limit = {

					}

				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_government = national_populist }

						NOT = {
							has_completed_focus = ITA_REP_nationalist_question
							has_completed_focus = ITA_REP_stable_democracy
						}
					}

				}

					remove_ideas = ITA_federation_transition
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = ITA_federation_secure }
					remove_ideas = ITA_federation_secure
				}
			}
		}

country_event = { #Offering land in Italy in exchange for faction membership
	id = annex.281
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.281" }
	title = annex.281.t

	desc = {
		text = annex.281.d.allitaly
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = offering_italy
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = annex.281.d.centralitaly
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = offering_papacy
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = annex.281.d.piedmont
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = offering_piedmont
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.281.a #We'll take the deal
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				FROM = { can_form_italy = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					tag = PAP
					tag = SRD
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_subject = no
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
					}
					country_event = annex.284
				}
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}

		separate_peace_all_wars = yes

		FROM = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = offering_italy } }
						is_european_italy = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = offering_papacy } }
						OR = {
							state = 764 #Viterbo
							state = 1005 #Umbria
							state = 157 #Marche
							state = 161 #Romagna
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = offering_piedmont } }
						OR = {
							state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
							state = 158 #Piedmont
							state = 838 #Liguria
							state = 762 #Nice
							state = 735 #Savoy
							state = 943 #Upper Savoy
						}
					}
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes
				}
				ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
			country_event = { id = annex.282 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.281.b #We refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				is_in_faction = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					has_war = yes
					tag = SIC
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = annex.283 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

					tag = AUS
					country_exists = VNC
					VNC = {
						has_country_flag = VNC_accepted_austrian_help
						has_country_flag = VNC_republican_revolt
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				SRD = { has_cosmetic_tag = SRD_ITA }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = ITA
					tag = SRI
					tag = SIC
					tag = SRD
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = LOM_CONQ

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SRD modifier = KR_returned_land }

		SRD = { transfer_state = 159 }
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.285.b #Give to VNC
		trigger = {
			tag = AUS
			country_exists = VNC
			VNC = {
				has_country_flag = VNC_accepted_austrian_help
				has_country_flag = VNC_republican_revolt
			}
		}
		VNC = { transfer_state = 159 }
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.l #Occupy
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}

		}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_italian_tag = no
				OR = {
					ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = VNC_CONQ

		hidden_effect = {

			}

				is_core_of = VNC

	id = annex.287
	title = annexation_TUS_CONQ
	desc = annexation_TUS_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.287"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = TUS_CONQ
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.287.a #Release as TUS grand duchy
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			OR = {
				tag = AUS
				tag = GER
				tag = SRD
				tag = SIC
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_italian_tag = no
				OR = {
					ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = TUS_CONQ

		hidden_effect = {
			TUS = {
				add_state_core = 162
			}
		}

		TUS = { transfer_state = 162 }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = TUS modifier = KR_liberated_us }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TUS }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
				set_autonomy = {
					target = TUS
					autonomy_state = kr_federated_state
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						has_government = paternal_autocrat
					}
				}
				TUS = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.2 }
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				ITA = {
					exists = yes
					has_country_leader = {

					SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}

			}
		}

		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TUS }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

country_event = { #The Fate of Piedmont
	id = annex.291
	title = annexation_PIEDMONT_CONQ
	desc = annexation_PIEDMONT_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.291"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.280.b #Release as SRI
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
			NOT = {
				is_italian_tag = yes
				country_exists = SRI
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_italian_tag = no
				OR = {
					ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ

		# restore initial cores if they were removed
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
						state = 158 #Piedmont
						state = 838 #Liguria
						state = 1004 #Emilia
						state = 161 #Romagna
						state = 162 #Tuscany
						state = 157 #Marches
						state = 1005 #Umbria
						state = 764 #Viterbo
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = SRI }
					remove_claim_by = SRI
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = SRI } }
					add_core_of = SRI
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
					state = 158 #Piedmont
					state = 838 #Liguria
					state = 1004 #Emilia
					state = 161 #Romagna
					state = 162 #Tuscany
					state = 157 #Marches
					state = 1005 #Umbria
					state = 764 #Viterbo
					state = 762 #Nice
					state = 735 #Savoy
					state = 943 #Upper Savoy
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SRI = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SRI modifier = KR_liberated_us }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SRI }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.291.a #Release as SRD
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = {
				country_exists = SRD
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_italian_tag = no
				OR = {
					ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ

		# restore initial cores if they were removed
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 1002 #Sassari
						state = 114 #Cagliari
						state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
						state = 158 #Piedmont
						state = 838 #Liguria
						state = 762 #Nice
						state = 735 #Savoy
						state = 943 #Upper Savoy
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = SRD }
					remove_claim_by = SRD
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = SRD } }
					add_core_of = SRD
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
					state = 158 #Piedmont
					state = 838 #Liguria
					state = 1002 #Sassari
					state = 114 #Cagliari
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SRD = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SRD }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = SRD
				autonomy_state = kr_federated_state
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SRD = {
					owns_state = 158
					NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = SRD_piedmont }
				}
			}
			SRD = { set_cosmetic_tag = SRD_piedmont }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				SRD = {
					NOT = { owns_state = 158 }
					has_cosmetic_tag = SRD_piedmont
				}
			}
			SRD = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
		}

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SRD modifier = KR_liberated_us }
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.i #Offer to SRD
		trigger = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			has_socialist_government = no
			838 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SRD = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				controls_all_owned_states = yes
				has_socialist_government = no
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = offered_piedmont_@ROOT }
			}
			NOT = {
				ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				SRD = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				SIC = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}

				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				OR = {
					state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
					state = 158 #Piedmont
					state = 838 #Liguria
					state = 762 #Nice
					state = 735 #Savoy
					state = 943 #Upper Savoy
				}
			}
			SRD = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.h #Make a deal with SRD
		trigger = {
			tag = SIC
			owns_state = 838
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SIC_empire }
			controls_all_owned_states = yes
			SRD = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				controls_all_owned_states = yes
			}

		SRD = { country_event = sic.100 }

		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes

country_event = { #The Fate of Sardinia
	id = annex.292
	title = annexation_SRD_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SRD_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.292"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SRD_CONQ
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.292.a #Release as SRD
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = { country_exists = SRD }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_italian_tag = no
				OR = {
					ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = SRD_CONQ

		# restore initial cores if they were removed
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 1002 #Sassari
						state = 114 #Cagliari
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = SRD }
					remove_claim_by = SRD
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = SRD } }
					add_core_of = SRD
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
						state = 158 #Piedmont
						state = 838 #Liguria
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_claimed_by = SRD
							is_core_of = SRD
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = SRD
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1002 #Sassari
					state = 114 #Cagliari
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SRD = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SRD }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = SRD
				autonomy_state = kr_federated_state
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SRD = {
					owns_state = 158
					NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = SRD_piedmont }
				}
			}
			SRD = { set_cosmetic_tag = SRD_piedmont }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				SRD = {
					NOT = { owns_state = 158 }
					has_cosmetic_tag = SRD_piedmont
				}
			}
			SRD = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
		}

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SRD modifier = KR_liberated_us }
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.c #Give to ITA allies
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = ITA }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
			ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		clr_country_flag = SRD_CONQ

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = KR_returned_land }

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1002 #Sassari
					state = 114 #Cagliari
				}
			}
			ITA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.e #Give to SRI allies
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = SRI }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
			SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		clr_country_flag = SRD_CONQ

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SRI modifier = KR_returned_land }

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1002 #Sassari
					state = 114 #Cagliari
				}
			}
			SRI = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.f #Give to SIC allies
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = SIC }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
			SIC = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {

			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = SRD_CONQ

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SIC modifier = KR_returned_land }

		every_owned_state = {

					state = 114 #Cagliari

			SIC = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {

		}

	title = annexation_DDR_CONQ

			}
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
		}
	}

						amount = 4

						63 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes }
						64 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes }
						65 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes }
						66 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes }
						68 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		create_prussian_cores = yes
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = DDR }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { tag = RUS }
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { has_socialist_government = no } }
				DDR = { country_event = part.19 }
			}
			else = {
				DDR = { country_event = part.51 }
			}
		}
			if = {
				limit = {

					}

				country_event = { id = part.572 days = 2 }
				}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = BOL } }
				add_core_of = BOL
			}
			BOL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.333.b #Split it between PAR and BOL
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 1027
			owns_state = 688
			PAR = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
			BOL = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				BOL = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				PAR = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				BOL = { is_ally_of_ROOT = no }
				PAR = { is_ally_of_ROOT = no }
			}
		}
		688 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = PAR }
				remove_claim_by = PAR
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = PAR } }
				add_core_of = PAR
			}
			PAR = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		1027 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = BOL }
				remove_claim_by = BOL
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = BOL } }
				add_core_of = BOL
			}
			BOL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		set_country_flag = PAR_CHACO_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

	desc = annexation_EASTPRUSSIA_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

		name = annex.340.a
		trigger = {
			is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no

			}

		ai_chance = {

			modifier = {

			}

		5 = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes } #East Prussia

		name = annex.340.b
		trigger = {
			is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
			NOT = { tag = POL }

				POL = { owns_state = 777 }
				777 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Masuria
			}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {

					ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
				}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = POL }

				}
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
		}
	}

				is_germany_or_splinter_tag = yes
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 63.owner }
		5 = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes }
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line

		777 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
	}

	option = { #Annex East Prussia
		name = annex.340.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = POL
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					has_government = national_populist
					var:63.owner = { is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no }
					var:63.owner = { ROOT_can_grant_land = no }
				}
			}
		}
		add_state_claim = 5
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.1005.c
		trigger = {
			is_germany_or_splinter_tag = yes
		}

			base = 1000
		}
		add_state_core = 5
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy

		trigger = {

			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = no
			NOT = { tag = POL }

		occupy_small_country = yes

	}

		name = annex.341.a
		trigger = {
			is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
			NOT = { tag = POL }
			POL = {
				owns_state = 98 #Plock
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = POL }
		777 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
	}

	option = { #Give it to the Germans
		name = annex.342.a
		trigger = {
			is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
			NOT = { tag = POL }
			var:5.owner = {
				is_germany_or_splinter_tag = yes
				is_ally_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = ENG
					is_french_tag = yes
					is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
				}
				POL = {
					owns_state = 98 #Plock
					ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				POL = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 5.owner }
		777 = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes }
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.1005.c
		trigger = {
			is_germany_or_splinter_tag = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1000
		}
		add_state_core = 777
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			tag = POL
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1000
		}
		add_state_claim = 777
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
			OR = {
			10 = { is_claimed_by = ROOT } #== RUS has annexed Poland

			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1000
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				10 = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
			}
		POL = { add_state_core = 777 }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_germany_or_splinter_tag = no
			NOT = {
				tag = POL
				AND = {
					is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
					10 = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = MASURIA_CONQ
	}
}

				tag = POL
			}

					}
				}
			}

					owns_state = 189 #Samogitia

					}

			}
		}

				AND = {
					owns_state = 189 #Samogitia
					OR = {

						is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
					}
				}
				AND = {
					tag = POL

				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = MEMEL_CONQ
	}
}

				var:tag_to_release = {
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = 0
						syndicalist = 0
						social_democrat = 0
						social_liberal = 0
						market_liberal = 10
						social_conservative = 10
						authoritarian_democrat = 16
						paternal_autocrat = 59
						national_populist = 5
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #give to ARA ally
		name = annex.366.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = JBS
				tag = HEJ
				tag = SAU
			}
			var:656.owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = JBS
					tag = HEJ
					tag = SAU
				}
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { is_ally_with = 656.owner }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 656.owner }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				OR = {
					state = 907 #Bahrain
					state = 993 #Qatar
					state = 658 #Abu Dhabi
				}
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_core = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #split ARA/PER
		name = annex.366.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = JBS
				tag = HEJ
				tag = SAU
				tag = PER
			}
			var:656.owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = JBS
					tag = HEJ
					tag = SAU
				}
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
			}
			907 = { #Bahrain
				is_valid_annexation_state = yes
				is_claimed_by = PER
			}
			PER = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { is_ally_with = PER }
			}
		}
		PER = { transfer_state = 907 } #Bahrain
		
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 656.owner }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				OR = {
					state = 993 #Qatar
					state = 658 #Abu Dhabi
				}
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_core = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = JBS
				tag = HEJ
				tag = SAU
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				OR = {
					state = 907 #Bahrain
					state = 993 #Qatar
					state = 658 #Abu Dhabi
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			NOT = {
				tag = JBS
				tag = HEJ
				tag = SAU
			}
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = TRU_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of the Suez Canal
	id = annex.367
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.367" }
	title = annexation_SUEZ_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SUEZ_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Set up an international zone
		name = annex.367.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = PAL }
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = GBR
					tag = NFA
					tag = GER
					tag = RUS
					has_authoritarian_government = yes
				}
			}
		}
		save_global_event_target_as = canal_zone_main_patron
		OTT_set_up_suez_canal_zone = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Return it to EGY
		name = annex.367.b
		trigger = {
			EGY = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = GBR
					tag = NFA
					tag = GER
					tag = RUS
					has_authoritarian_government = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_actual_major = yes
				has_socialist_government = no
			}
		}
		EGY = { transfer_state = 753 }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Return it to OTT
		name = annex.367.c
		trigger = {
			TUR = {
				owns_state = 453
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = GBR
					tag = NFA
					tag = GER
					tag = RUS
					has_authoritarian_government = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_actual_major = yes
				has_socialist_government = no
			}
		}
		TUR = {
			add_state_core = 753
			transfer_state = 753
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Keep it
		name = annex.367.d
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		set_country_flag = SUEZ_CONQ
	}
}

					tag = SRD
					tag = VNC
				}
				is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			NOT = {

				tag = CRO
				tag = ITA

				tag = SRD
				tag = VNC
			}

				}

				}

			}

					is_in_faction_with = VNC
					VNC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					state = 1206
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = VNC }
					remove_claim_by = VNC
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = VNC } }
					add_core_of = VNC
				}
				VNC = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			VNC = {
				country_event = annex.18
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = SRD
					SRD = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					state = 1206
				}

					remove_claim_by = SRD
				}

					add_core_of = SRD
				}
				SRD = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			SRD = {
				country_event = annex.18
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = SIC
					SIC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					state = 1206
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = SIC }
					remove_claim_by = SIC
				}
				if = {

					add_core_of = SIC
				}
				SIC = { transfer_state = PREV }

				}

				}
				if = {

				}
				if = {

					add_core_of = SRI
				}
				SRI = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}

				country_event = annex.18
			}
		}

				tag = CRO

				}
			}

		}

			factor = 1000
		}

				state = 1230 #Starodub
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				add_core_of = UKR
				start_resistance = UKR
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = UKR
				tag = WHR
				AND = {
					tag = LIT
					owns_state = 206
				}
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = UKR }
			}
			add_state_claim = 1230
			if = {
				limit = {
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
			}
			add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 1230 }
			hidden_effect = {
				1230 = { add_core_of = UKR }
				1230 = { start_resistance = UKR }
			}
		}
		}
		else = {
			add_state_core = 1230
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
				tag = UKR
				AND = {
					tag = LIT
					206 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Minsk
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = STARODUB_CONQ
	}
}

		hidden_effect = {

						OR = {
							state = 234
							state = 235
							state = 1227
							state = 1190
						}
					}
				}
				KUB = { remove_state_core = PREV }
			}
		}
	}
	title = annexation_KUB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_KUB_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet

			base = 20

				factor = 0
				is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes

			}

					elections_allowed = no
				}

			}
			KUB = {

					ruling_party = social_conservative
					elections_allowed = no
				}

					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 40
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Form Don-Kuban Union
		name = annex.168.e

			tag = DKB
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = DKB }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = KUB
				}

			}

			NOT = { tag = DKB }

			base = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = KUB
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = KUB
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		occupy_tiny_country = yes
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = KUB }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

		}

		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ROOT.tag_to_release = THIS }
			}
		}
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

			NOT = { tag = DKB }
		}

			base = 0
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = KUB_CONQ
	}

				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = WSU }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #Occupy West Ukraine
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = POL
				tag = UKR
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					AUS_is_unified = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = WSU_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Northern Manchuria
	id = annex.405
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.405 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = annexation_NORTHERN_MANCHURIA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_NORTHERN_MANCHURIA_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.405"
		determine_chinese_ally = yes
	}

	option = { #Release Independent Manchuria
		name = annex.178.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = MAN }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 85
				tag = JAP
				}
			}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = MAN }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 883 #Shenyang
						state = 884
						state = 885
						state = 714
						state = 717
					}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			var:tag_to_release = {
				add_state_core = PREV
				transfer_state = PREV
				}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = JAP }
				hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = MAN }
				puppet_released_tag = yes
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = MAN
				autonomy_state = kr_special_autonomous_dependency
					}
			MAN = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = market_liberal
					elections_allowed = no
					}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = 0
						syndicalist = 0
						social_democrat = 2
						social_liberal = 6
						market_liberal = 47
						social_conservative = 12
						authoritarian_democrat = 15
						paternal_autocrat = 6
						national_populist = 12
					}
				}
				}
			}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = MAN }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Release China
		name = annex.174.a
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = china_release_target
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = event_target:china_release_target }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
			OR = {
					state = 883 #Shenyang
					state = 884
					state = 885
					state = 714
					state = 717
				}
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			add_claim_by = var:tag_to_release
			transfer_state_to = var:tag_to_release
		}
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { var:tag_to_release = { tag = FNG } }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = var:tag_to_release
				autonomy_state = kr_special_autonomous_dependency
				end_wars = no
				}
			}
		var:tag_to_release = { china_puppet_setup = yes }
			}
	
	option = { #Give to a Chinese ally
		name = annex.174.c
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = china_ally_target
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = event_target:china_ally_target modifier = KR_returned_land }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 883 #Shenyang
					state = 884
					state = 885
					state = 714
					state = 717
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { tag = JAP } }
					NOT = { has_variable = ambition_area_@ROOT }
				}
			}
			transfer_state_to = event_target:china_ally_target
		}
			}
	
	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.integration
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag_that_can_integrate = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				var:716.owner = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 883 #Shenyang
					state = 884
					state = 885
					state = 714
					state = 717
			}
			}
			add_claim_of_ROOT = yes
			add_core_of = MAN
			start_resistance = MAN
		}
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 883 }
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 884 }
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 885 }
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 714 }
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_state_array = 717 }
		add_political_power = -50
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = NORTHERN_MANCHURIA_CONQ
	}
}
